## 2026-06-15

### 1

- 日期：2026-06-15
- 时间戳：无时间戳
- 原句：Oil reserves around the world have been drawn down, some to their lowest ever levels.
- 慢速拆解：Oil reserves / around the world / have been drawn down / some to their lowest ever levels.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：`have been` 弱读成很轻的功能块；`drawn down` 两个重音词要读清。
- 中文意思：全球石油储备已经被消耗，有些降到历史最低水平。
- 跟读次数建议：8 次

### 2

- 日期：2026-06-15
- 时间戳：无时间戳
- 原句：This whole conflict and the closure of the Strait of Hormuz has exposed how vulnerable we are to the supply shocks.
- 慢速拆解：This whole conflict / and the closure of the Strait of Hormuz / has exposed / how vulnerable we are / to the supply shocks.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：`of the` 很轻；`has exposed` 容易连在一起；专名 `Hormuz` 单独练。
- 中文意思：这场冲突和霍尔木兹海峡关闭暴露了我们面对供应冲击时有多脆弱。
- 跟读次数建议：10 次

### 3

- 日期：2026-06-15
- 时间戳：无时间戳
- 原句：You can't just, once you've shut oil or gas field in, you can't just switch it on overnight.
- 慢速拆解：You can't just / once you've shut oil or gas field in / you can't just switch it on / overnight.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：`can't just` 中 `t` 可能弱化；`switch it on` 有明显连读。
- 中文意思：油气田关闭后，不可能一夜之间重新开启。
- 跟读次数建议：10 次

### 4

- 日期：2026-06-15
- 时间戳：无时间戳
- 原句：The RBA has to sit still for an extended period while it puts downward pressure on the economy.
- 慢速拆解：The RBA / has to sit still / for an extended period / while it puts downward pressure / on the economy.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：`has to` 可弱读为 /hæstə/；`for an` 连读；`on the` 弱读。
- 中文意思：澳洲央行需要较长时间维持不动，从而对经济施加下行压力。
- 跟读次数建议：8 次

### 5

- 日期：2026-06-15
- 时间戳：无时间戳
- 原句：Details are scarce, but a draft 14-point plan leaked by Iranian state media suggests the deal could include reopening of the Strait of Hormuz within 30 days.
- 慢速拆解：Details are scarce / but a draft 14-point plan / leaked by Iranian state media / suggests the deal could include / reopening of the Strait of Hormuz / within 30 days.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：数字 `14-point` 和 `30 days` 要重读；`could include` 中 `could` 弱读。
- 中文意思：细节很少，但伊朗官方媒体泄露的 14 点草案显示，协议可能包括 30 天内重开霍尔木兹海峡。
- 跟读次数建议：12 次

### 6

- 日期：2026-06-15
- 时间戳：无时间戳
- 原句：We'd expect that to flow through to the bowsers, but let's see if it's sustained.
- 慢速拆解：We'd expect that / to flow through / to the bowsers / but let's see / if it's sustained.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：`We'd expect` 开头压缩；`to the` 弱读；`if it's` 连读。
- 中文意思：我们预计这会传导到加油站价格，但还要看能否持续。
- 跟读次数建议：10 次

### 7

- 日期：2026-06-15
- 时间戳：无时间戳
- 原句：The Socceroos and their fans are still basking in the afterglow of the team's 2-0 win.
- 慢速拆解：The Socceroos and their fans / are still basking / in the afterglow / of the team's 2-0 win.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：`and their` 弱读；`in the afterglow` 连成一个意群；`2-0` 读作 two-nil。
- 中文意思：澳大利亚男足和球迷仍沉浸在球队 2-0 获胜后的喜悦中。

### 8

- 日期：2026-06-15
- 时间戳：无时间戳
- 原句：Some technology companies want us to think that social media is unchangeable, part of an almost natural order.
- 慢速拆解：Some technology companies / want us to think / that social media is unchangeable / part of an almost natural order.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：`want us to` 常被压缩；`part of an` 连读；抽象名词要按意群读。
- 中文意思：一些科技公司想让我们以为社交媒体不可改变，几乎像自然秩序的一部分。

## 2026-06-17

### 1

- 日期：2026-06-17
- 时间戳：05:20–05:40
- 原句：This is just a ceasefire that will come before a longer peace process, and the more sticky questions around Iran's nuclear program and the future of the Strait of Hormuz are just beginning to be negotiated now.
- 慢速拆解：This is just a ceasefire / that will come before a longer peace process / and the more sticky questions / around Iran's nuclear program / and the future of the Strait of Hormuz / are just beginning to be negotiated now.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：根据常见发音规律，`this is just a`、`that will`、`are just beginning to be` 会明显压缩；`Strait of Hormuz` 单独练音形。
- 中文意思：这只是长期和平进程之前的一次停火，围绕伊朗核计划和霍尔木兹海峡未来的棘手问题才刚开始谈判。
- 跟读次数建议：12 次

### 2

- 日期：2026-06-17
- 时间戳：06:00–06:20
- 原句：The United States has walked back a few of its red lines and has made a number of concessions to Iran to get it over the line.
- 慢速拆解：The United States / has walked back a few of its red lines / and has made a number of concessions to Iran / to get it over the line.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：`has walked back` 和 `has made a` 中功能词可能很轻；重读 `walked back`、`red lines`、`concessions`、`over the line`。
- 中文意思：美国放宽了部分原有底线，并对伊朗作出一些让步，以最终促成协议。
- 跟读次数建议：10 次

- 时间戳：09:20–09:40
- 原句：We need to broaden our understanding of what economic security is and understand that economic interconnectedness is creating avenues for weaponisation as well.
- 慢速拆解：We need to broaden our understanding / of what economic security is / and understand / that economic interconnectedness / is creating avenues for weaponisation as well.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：长抽象词要保持重音清楚；`of what`、`and understand that`、`for weaponisation` 可能连读或弱读。
- 中文意思：我们需要扩大对经济安全的理解，并认识到经济互联也在创造被武器化利用的渠道。

- 连读 / 弱读提示：`might all`、`from this`、`if we would` 可能压缩；重读对比 `more good / less evil / too much`。
- 中文意思：如果注意不要为欲望付出过高代价，我们都能从世界获得更多好处、少受一些痛苦。
- 跟读次数建议：10 次

- 慢速拆解：You are young / and have the world before you / stoop / as you go through it / and you will miss / many hard thumps.

- 中文意思：你还年轻，世界就在前方；一路上懂得低头谦逊，就能避开许多沉重打击。

- 连读 / 弱读提示：`utility of this`、`by time and experience`、`to be much disputed` 可能压缩；重读主干 `utility / became evident / disputed`。
- 中文意思：这种纸币的效用经时间和经验变得非常明显，后来几乎不再受到质疑。
- 跟读次数建议：14 次

- 慢速拆解：I took care / not only to be in reality / industrious and frugal / but to avoid / all appearances / to the contrary.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：必须强读 `not only / but`；`to be in reality` 和 `appearances to the contrary` 容易连成一串。
- 中文意思：我不仅真正勤劳节俭，也避免给人留下相反的印象。

- 慢速拆解：While Washington was / the animating spirit / of the struggle in the colonies / Franklin was / its ablest champion abroad.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：按 Washington / Franklin 两端对称分拍；`ablest` 不要读成 `ableist`。
- 中文意思：Washington 是殖民地内部斗争的核心推动者，而 Franklin 是海外最有力的倡导者。

- 慢速拆解：GPSR uses greedy forwarding / while a closer neighbour is available / and switches / to perimeter forwarding / when it reaches a void.
- 连读 / 弱读提示：GPSR 逐字母读；重读两个 mode 和触发条件 `when it reaches a void`。
- 中文意思：有更近邻居时 GPSR 使用贪心转发，遇到空洞时切换到周界转发。
- 跟读次数建议：20 次
